  <script>
   var loadingTaboola  = false;
var TaboolaInterval = null;

let AdsLaunched = false;
let AdsInterval;
let cmpCheckInterval;

window.cmpAccepted = false;

function CheckAdsLaunched()
{
  if(!AdsLaunched)
  {
    AdsLaunched = true;
    window.cmpAccepted = true;

    InitDailyMotionInHome();

    AdsInterval =  setInterval(function(){  
      if (typeof StartAdManagerAndPrebid !== "undefined") { 
          clearInterval(AdsInterval);
          StartAdManagerAndPrebid();
      }
    }, 1000);
  }
}

function InitDailyMotionInHome()
{
  let videoList = document.querySelectorAll(".video--home--trigger");
  var videoListArray = [...videoList];

  videoListArray.forEach(div =>
  {
    try
    {
        div.addEventListener("click", () => 
        { 
            div.style.pointerEvents = "none";

            const pageURL = div.querySelector("iframe").src;
            const videoID = pageURL.substr(pageURL.lastIndexOf('/') + 1).split("?")[0];
            const player  = DM.player(div.querySelector('.video--external'), { video: videoID });

            player.load(videoID,
            {
                autoplay: true,
                start: 0
            });
        });
    }
    catch(err)
    {

    }
  });
}
  </script>

  <script data-cookieconsent="marketing">
   var extid = ("; " + document.cookie).split("; dldtx=").pop().split(";").shift();
    document.write('<scr'+'ipt type="text/javascript" src="https://dmp.citiservi.es/dtpx.js?acc=2504&p=ubmmikwz&m=3&id=' + extid+'" ></scr'+'ipt>');

  <script async="async" src="https://www.googletagservices.com/tag/js/gpt.js">
  </script>
  <script>
   function getAdUnitsRaiPlacement (adUnitName){
		return raiPlacementObj.find(x=>x.adUnit == adUnitName) || false;
	}

	function seedtagDomain()
	{
		if(location.href.includes("muyinteresante"))
		{
			return { "adUnit": "20650348", "publisher": "3301-3619-01" };
		}

		if(location.href.includes("marie-claire"))
		{
			return { "adUnit": "20650344", "publisher": "5347-1275-01" };
		}

		if(location.href.includes("serpadres"))
		{
			return { "adUnit": "20650346", "publisher": "8591-4263-01" };
		}

		return null;
	}

	function raiAddAdUnits(adSlots) {
	    pbAdUnits = adSlots.map(function(slot) 
		{
			const elementName = slot.name.replace('/21614288668/', '');
			const seedtagID = seedtagDomain(elementName);

			raiPlacement = getAdUnitsRaiPlacement(elementName);

			if(isMobileDevice && elementName.includes("sticky") && (seedtagID != null))
			{
				return {code: slot.name, mediaTypes: {banner: {sizes: raiPlacement[deviceType].sizes}}, sizes: raiPlacement[deviceType].sizes, 
				bids: 
				[
					{ bidder: 'seedtag', params: { adUnitId: seedtagID.adUnit, publisherId: seedtagID.publisher, placement: 'inScreen' }},
					{ bidder: 'richaudience', params: { pid: raiPlacement.raiPlacement, supplyType: 'site' }},
					{ bidder: 'rubicon', params: { accountId: '17386', siteId: getSiteID(), zoneId: raiPlacement.rcZoneID }}
				]};
			}
			else
			{
				return {code: slot.name, mediaTypes: {banner: {sizes: raiPlacement[deviceType].sizes}}, sizes: raiPlacement[deviceType].sizes, 
				bids: 
				[
					{ bidder: 'richaudience', params: { pid: raiPlacement.raiPlacement, supplyType: 'site' }},
					{ bidder: 'rubicon', params: { accountId: '17386', siteId: getSiteID(), zoneId: raiPlacement.rcZoneID }}
				]};
			}
		});
	}

	function raiRemoveAdUnits() {
            pbjs.removeAdUnit();
            pbAdUnits = [];
            adSlots = [];
	}

	function raiCallSlots(){
            pbjs.initAdserverSet = false;
            pbjs.addAdUnits(pbAdUnits);
            pbjs.requestBids({
                bidsBackHandler: initAdserver,
                timeout: PREBID_TIMEOUT
            });
	}

	function getGoogleTagByAdUnitPath (adUnitName) {
		var googleTagArray = googletag.pubads().getSlots();
		for (i = 0; i < googleTagArray.length; i++) {
	        if (googleTagArray[i].getAdUnitPath() === adUnitName) {
				return googleTagArray[i];
			}
	    }
	    return;
	}

	function getNameForRefresh(name)
	{
		let googleTagArray = googletag.pubads().getSlots();
		let tmpSlot = undefined;

		googleTagArray.forEach( slot => {
			if(slot.getSlotElementId() == name)
				tmpSlot = slot;
		});

		return tmpSlot;
	}

	function getNameForRefreshDynamic(slot)
	{
		let googleTagArray = googletag.pubads().getSlots();
		let tmpSlot = undefined;

		googleTagArray.forEach( slotItem =>
		{
			if(slot.name.includes("mega"))
			{
				if(slotItem. getSlotElementId() == "mega2_" + slot.indexResto)
					tmpSlot = slotItem;
			}

			if(slot.name.includes("roba"))
			{
				if(slotItem. getSlotElementId() == "roba1_" + slot.indexResto)
					tmpSlot = slotItem;
			}
		});

		return tmpSlot;
	}

	function initAdserver() {
		if (pbjs.initAdserverSet) return;
		pbjs.initAdserverSet = true;
		googletag.cmd.push(function() {
			pbjs.setTargetingForGPTAsync && pbjs.setTargetingForGPTAsync();

			adSlots.map(function(slot) {
				var renderAdSlot;

				if(slot.name.includes("resto"))
				{
					renderAdSlot = getNameForRefreshDynamic(slot);
				}
				else
				{
					renderAdSlot = getGoogleTagByAdUnitPath(slot.name);
				}

				if (renderAdSlot != undefined) {
					googletag.pubads().refresh([renderAdSlot]);
				}
			});
		});
	}

	// AdsLaunched

    function PaintPrebidAds(elements)
    {
		if(!pbjs || typeof pbjs.removeAdUnit !== "function")
		{
            console.log("pbjs not loaded or pbjs.removeAdUnit not available");
			setTimeout(() => { PaintPrebidAds(elements) }, 3000);
			return;
		}

		raiRemoveAdUnits();

		elements.forEach( (item) => {

			if(PrebidNamesMap.has(item.name))
			{
				if(item.index === -2)
				{
					if(item.name.includes("sticky"))
					{
						adSlots.push( {name: `/21614288668/muyinteresante/` + PrebidNamesMap.get(item.name)} );
					}
					else
					{
						if(!IsPainted(`/21614288668/muyinteresante/` + PrebidNamesMap.get(item.name)))
							adSlots.push( {name: `/21614288668/muyinteresante/` + PrebidNamesMap.get(item.name)} );
					}

					return;
				}

				if(item.index === 0)
				{
					if(!IsPainted(`/21614288668/dynamic_1/` + PrebidNamesMap.get(item.name)))
						adSlots.push( {name: `/21614288668/dynamic_1/` + PrebidNamesMap.get(item.name)} );

					return;
				}

				if(item.index < 0)
				{
					if(!IsPainted('/21614288668/muyinteresante/' + PrebidNamesMap.get(item.name)))
						adSlots.push( {name: '/21614288668/muyinteresante/' + PrebidNamesMap.get(item.name)} );

					return;
				}

				if(item.index >=1 && item.index <= 5)
				{
					if(!IsPainted(`/21614288668/dynamic_${item.index}/` + PrebidNamesMap.get(item.name)))
						adSlots.push( {name: `/21614288668/dynamic_${item.index}/` + PrebidNamesMap.get(item.name)} );
				}

				if(item.index > 5)
				{
					if(!IsPainted(`/21614288668/dynamic_resto/` + PrebidNamesMap.get(item.name) + "_" + item.index))
					{
						GenerateDynamicSlotPrebid(item.name, item.index);
						adSlots.push( {name: `/21614288668/dynamic_resto/` + PrebidNamesMap.get(item.name), indexResto: item.index} );
					}
				}
			}
		});

		raiAddAdUnits(adSlots);

		raiCallSlots();
    }

	function IsPainted(item)
	{
		if(RefreshedItems.has(item))
		{
			return true;
		}
		else
		{
			RefreshedItems.add(item);
			return false;
		}
	}

    function CreateDynamicInContent(elementId)
    {
        let slot = googletag.defineSlot('/21614288668/muyinteresante/in_content', [[1, 1], [300, 250], [300, 600], 'fluid'], elementId).defineSizeMapping(dynamicInContent).addService(googletag.pubads());
        gptadslots.push(slot);

		googletag.display(elementId);
		googletag.pubads().refresh([slot]);
    }

	function GenerateAndPaintDynamicButtons(index)
	{
		if(RefreshedItems.has('button1_' + index) || RefreshedItems.has('button2_' + index) || RefreshedItems.has('button3_' + index))
		{
			return;
		}
		else
		{
			RefreshedItems.add('button1_' + index);
			RefreshedItems.add('button2_' + index);
			RefreshedItems.add('button3_' + index);
		}

		let slotButton1 = googletag.defineSlot('/21614288668/dynamic_resto/button_1', [[1, 1], [320, 50], [320, 100]], 'button1_' + index).defineSizeMapping(getDynamicMapping("button")[1]).addService(googletag.pubads());
		let slotButton2 = googletag.defineSlot('/21614288668/dynamic_resto/button_2', [[1, 1], [320, 50], [320, 100]], 'button2_' + index).defineSizeMapping(getDynamicMapping("button")[1]).addService(googletag.pubads());
		let slotButton3 = googletag.defineSlot('/21614288668/dynamic_resto/button_3', [[1, 1], [320, 50], [320, 100]], 'button3_' + index).defineSizeMapping(getDynamicMapping("button")[1]).addService(googletag.pubads());

		gptadslots.push(slotButton1);
		gptadslots.push(slotButton2);
		gptadslots.push(slotButton3);

		googletag.cmd.push(function() {
			googletag.display('button1_' + index);
			googletag.display('button2_' + index);
			googletag.display('button3_' + index);
		});

		googletag.pubads().refresh([slotButton1, slotButton2, slotButton3]);
	}

	function GenerateDynamicSlotPrebid(name, index)
	{
		if(name.includes("mega"))
		{
			googletag.cmd.push(function() {
				googletag.defineSlot('/21614288668/dynamic_resto/mega', [[1, 1], [320, 50], [320, 100]], 'mega2_' + index ).defineSizeMapping(getDynamicMapping("mega")[1]).addService(googletag.pubads());
				googletag.pubads().enableSingleRequest();
				googletag.enableServices();
			});
		}

		if(name.includes("roba"))
		{
			googletag.cmd.push(function() {
				googletag.defineSlot('/21614288668/dynamic_resto/roba', [[1, 1], [320, 50], [320, 100]], 'roba1_' + index).defineSizeMapping(getDynamicMapping("roba")[1]).addService(googletag.pubads());
				googletag.pubads().enableSingleRequest();
				googletag.enableServices();
			});
		}
	}

    function getDynamicMapping(elementId)
    {
        if (elementId.includes("roba")) {
            return ['roba', dynamicRobaSize];
        }
        if (elementId.includes("mega")) {
            return ['mega', dynamicMegaSize];
        }
        if (elementId.includes("button")) {
            index = elementId.match(/button([0-9])_/);
            return ['button', dynamicButtonSize];
        }
    }

    function CreateMutator(element)
    {
        if(!location.href.includes("delooks"))
            return;

        if(element.includes("sticky"))
            return;

        const tmpMutator = new MutationObserver(DetectMutationInAdsContainers);
        tmpMutator.observe(document.querySelector("#" + element), config);

        setTimeout(()=> { console.log("No change in: " + tmpMutator); tmpMutator.disconnect(); }, MutatorTimeuot);
    }

	function DetectMutationInAdsContent(mutationsList, observer)
	{
		for(let mutation of mutationsList)
		{
			if (mutation.type === 'attributes' && mutation.attributeName === "data-load-complete")
			{
				observer.disconnect();

				setTimeout( ()=>
				{
					try
					{
						const size = mutation.target.contentWindow.document.querySelector("body").getBoundingClientRect();

						if(+size.height < 50)
						{
							if(!mutation.target.closest("[data-google-query-id]").parentNode.querySelector("#floating_item_top"))
							{
								console.log("Collapsing: " + mutation.target.parentNode.id + " size: " + size.height);
								mutation.target.closest("[data-google-query-id]").parentNode.style.display = "none";
							}
						}
					}
					catch(err)
					{
						console.log("Error accessing iframe from mutator");
					}
				}, 2000);
			}
		}
	}

	function DetectMutationInAdsContainers(mutationsList, observer)
	{
		for(let mutation of mutationsList)
		{
			if (mutation.type === 'attributes' && mutation.attributeName === "data-google-query-id")
			{
				observer.disconnect();

				let tmpMutatorforADS = new MutationObserver(DetectMutationInAdsContent);
				let tmpIframe = mutation.target.querySelector("iframe");

				if(tmpIframe)
				{
					tmpMutatorforADS.observe(tmpIframe, config);
					setTimeout(() => { console.log("Cleaning mutator"); tmpMutatorforADS.disconnect(); }, MutatorTimeuot);
				}
			}
		}
	};

	function getSiteID()
	{
		if(deviceIsMobile)
			return "353274";
		else
			return "353216";

	}

	function StartAdManagerAndPrebid()
	{
		if(adsCalled)
			return;

		adsCalled = true;

		googletag.cmd.push(function() {
			googletag.pubads().disableInitialLoad();
		});

		pbjs.que.push(function() {
		pbjs.setConfig({
			consentManagement: {
			cmpApi: 'iab',
			timeout: 8000,
			allowAuctionWithoutConsent: false
			},
			userSync: {
				filterSettings: {
					iframe: {
						bidders: '*',
						filter: 'include'
					}
				}
			},
			enableSendAllBids: true,
			priceGranularity: "dense"
		});

		pbjs.addAdUnits(pbAdUnits);
		pbjs.requestBids({
			bidsBackHandler: initAdserver,
			timeout: PREBID_TIMEOUT
		});
		});

		setTimeout(function() {
			initAdserver;
		}, FAILSAFE_TIMEOUT);

		googletag.cmd.push(function ()
		{
			var mappingMega1 = googletag.sizeMapping()
				.addSize([1024, 0], sizesMega1Desktop)
				.addSize([970, 0], sizesMegaTablet)
				.addSize([0, 0], sizesMegaMobile)
				.build();

			var mappingMega2 = googletag.sizeMapping()
				.addSize([1024, 0], sizesMega2Desktop)
				.addSize([970, 0], sizesMegaTablet)
				.addSize([0, 0], sizesMegaMobile)
				.build();

			dynamicMegaSize = mappingMega2;

			var mappingRoba = googletag.sizeMapping()
				.addSize([0, 0], sizesRoba)
				.build();

			dynamicRobaSize = mappingRoba;

			var mappingRobaDesktop = googletag.sizeMapping()
				.addSize([1024, 0], sizesRoba)
				.addSize([0, 0], [])
				.build();
			var mappingRobaMobile = googletag.sizeMapping()
				.addSize([1024, 0], [])
				.addSize([0, 0], sizesRoba)
				.build();

			var mappingButton = googletag.sizeMapping()
				.addSize([0, 0], sizesButton)
				.build();

			dynamicButtonSize = mappingButton;

			var mappingButtonDesktop = googletag.sizeMapping()
				.addSize([1024, 0], sizesButton)
				.addSize([0, 0], [])
				.build();

			var mappingButtonMobile = googletag.sizeMapping()
				.addSize([1024, 0], [])
				.addSize([0, 0], sizesButton)
				.build();

			var mappingInContent = googletag.sizeMapping()
				.addSize([0, 0], sizesRoba)
				.build();

			dynamicInContent = mappingInContent;

			var mappingSticky = googletag.sizeMapping()
				.addSize([1024, 0], sizesStickyDesktop)
				.addSize([970, 0], sizesStickyTablet)
				.addSize([0, 0], sizesStickyMobile)
				.build();

			pageIsGallery = document.querySelector(".gallery--main");
			pageIsTest    = document.querySelector("div[data-type='test']");

			if(!pageIsTest && !pageIsGallery)
			{
				slotsToGenerate = [
					{ name: "mega_1", div: "mega1", type: "static", usedIn: ["all"], outOfPage: false, sizesArray: [[1, 1], [320, 50], [320, 100]], mapping: mappingMega1 },
					{ name: "mega_2", div: "mega2", type: "static", usedIn:["all"], outOfPage: false, sizesArray: [[1, 1], [320, 50], [320, 100]], mapping: mappingMega2 },
					{ name: "mpu_1", div: "roba1", type: "static", usedIn: ["desktop"], outOfPage: false, sizesArray: [[1, 1], [300, 250], [300, 600], 'fluid'], mapping: mappingRobaDesktop },
					{ name: "mpu_2", div: "roba2", type: "static", usedIn: ["desktop"], outOfPage: false, sizesArray: [[1, 1], [300, 250], [300, 600], 'fluid'], mapping: mappingRobaDesktop },
					{ name: "mpu_3", div: "roba3", type: "static", usedIn: ["desktop"], outOfPage: false, sizesArray: [[1, 1], [300, 250], [300, 600], 'fluid'], mapping: mappingRobaDesktop },
					{ name: "button_1", div: "button1", type: "static", usedIn: ["all"], outOfPage: false, sizesArray: [[300, 150], 'fluid'], mapping: mappingButtonDesktop },
					{ name: "button_2", div: "button2", type: "static", usedIn: ["all"], outOfPage: false, sizesArray: [[300, 150], 'fluid'], mapping: mappingButtonDesktop },
					{ name: "button_3", div: "button3", type: "static", usedIn: ["all"], outOfPage: false, sizesArray: [[300, 150], 'fluid'], mapping: mappingButtonDesktop },
					{ name: "sticky_wall", div: "sticky_wall", type: "static", usedIn: ["all"], outOfPage: false, sizesArray: [[1, 1], [248, 1000]] , mapping: mappingSticky },
					{ name: "mpu_1", div: "roba1_mobile", type: "static", usedIn: ["mobile", "tablet"], outOfPage: false, sizesArray: [[1, 1], [300, 250], [300, 600], 'fluid'] , mapping: mappingRobaMobile },
					{ name: "mpu_2", div: "roba2_mobile", type: "static", usedIn: ["mobile", "tablet"], outOfPage: false, sizesArray: [[1, 1], [300, 250], [300, 600], 'fluid'] , mapping: mappingRobaMobile },
					{ name: "mpu_3", div: "roba3_mobile", type: "static", usedIn: ["mobile", "tablet"], outOfPage: false, sizesArray: [[1, 1], [300, 250], [300, 600], 'fluid'] , mapping: mappingRobaMobile },
					{ name: "button_1", div: "button1_mobile", type: "static", usedIn: ["all"], outOfPage: false, sizesArray: [[300, 150], 'fluid'] , mapping: mappingButtonMobile },
					{ name: "button_2", div: "button2_mobile", type: "static", usedIn: ["all"], outOfPage: false, sizesArray: [[300, 150], 'fluid'] , mapping: mappingButtonMobile },
					{ name: "button_3", div: "button3_mobile", type: "static", usedIn: ["all"], outOfPage: false, sizesArray: [[300, 150], 'fluid'] , mapping: mappingButtonMobile },
					{ name: "outofcontent1", div: "outofcontent1", type: "static", usedIn: ["all"], outOfPage: true, sizesArray: null , mapping: null },
					{ name: "outofcontent2", div: "outofcontent2", type: "static", usedIn: ["all"], outOfPage: true, sizesArray: null , mapping: null },
				];
			}

			if(pageIsTest || pageIsGallery)
			{
				slotsToGenerate = [
					{ itemIndex: 0, name: "mega_1", div: "mega1", type: "static", usedIn: ["all"], outOfPage: false, sizesArray: [[1, 1], [320, 50], [320, 100]], mapping: mappingMega1 },
					{ itemIndex: 0, name: "sticky_wall", div: "sticky_wall", type: "static", usedIn: ["all"], outOfPage: false, sizesArray: [[1, 1], [248, 1000]] , mapping: mappingSticky },
					{ itemIndex: 0, name: `outofcontent1`, div: `outofcontent1`, type: "static", usedIn: ["all"], outOfPage: true, sizesArray: null , mapping: null },
					{ itemIndex: 0, name: `outofcontent2`, div: `outofcontent2`, type: "static", usedIn: ["all"], outOfPage: true, sizesArray: null , mapping: null }
				];

				for(let counterSlot = 1; counterSlot <= 5; counterSlot++)
				{
					slotsToGenerate.push({ itemIndex: counterSlot, name: `mega`, div: `mega2_${counterSlot}`, type: "dynamic", usedIn: ["all"], outOfPage: false, sizesArray: [[1, 1], [320, 50], [320, 100]] , mapping: mappingMega2 });
					slotsToGenerate.push({ itemIndex: counterSlot, name: `roba`, div: `roba1_${counterSlot}`, type: "dynamic", usedIn: ["all"], outOfPage: false, sizesArray: [[1, 1], [300, 250], [300, 600], 'fluid'] , mapping: mappingRoba });
					slotsToGenerate.push({ itemIndex: counterSlot, name: `button_1`, div: `button1_${counterSlot}`, type: "dynamic", usedIn: ["all"], outOfPage: false, sizesArray: [[300, 150], 'fluid'] , mapping: mappingButton });
					slotsToGenerate.push({ itemIndex: counterSlot, name: `button_2`, div: `button2_${counterSlot}`, type: "dynamic", usedIn: ["all"], outOfPage: false, sizesArray: [[300, 150], 'fluid'] , mapping: mappingButton });
					slotsToGenerate.push({ itemIndex: counterSlot, name: `button_3`, div: `button3_${counterSlot}`, type: "dynamic", usedIn: ["all"], outOfPage: false, sizesArray: [[300, 150], 'fluid'] , mapping: mappingButton });
				}
			}

			slotsToGenerate.forEach((slotItem) =>
			{
				try
				{
					if(slotItem.outOfPage)
					{
						gptadslots.push( googletag.defineOutOfPageSlot(`/${ProviderID}/${WebID}/${slotItem.name}`, slotItem.div).addService(googletag.pubads()));
					}
					else
					{
						if(slotItem.usedIn.includes("all") || slotItem.usedIn.includes(deviceType))
						{
							if(slotItem.type === "dynamic")
							{
								gptadslots.push( googletag.defineSlot(`/${ProviderID}/dynamic_${slotItem.itemIndex}/${slotItem.name}`, slotItem.sizesArray, slotItem.div).defineSizeMapping(slotItem.mapping).addService(googletag.pubads()));
							}

							if(slotItem.type === "dynamic_resto")
							{
								gptadslots.push( googletag.defineSlot(`/${ProviderID}/dynamic_resto/${slotItem.name}`, slotItem.sizesArray, slotItem.div).defineSizeMapping(slotItem.mapping).addService(googletag.pubads()));
							}

							if(slotItem.type === "static")
							{
								gptadslots.push( googletag.defineSlot(`/${ProviderID}/${WebID}/${slotItem.name}`, slotItem.sizesArray, slotItem.div).defineSizeMapping(slotItem.mapping).addService(googletag.pubads()));
							}
						}
					}
				}
				catch(e)
				{
					console.log(e);
				}
			});

			googletag.pubads().addEventListener('slotRequested', (event) =>
			{
				if(event.slot.getAdUnitPath().includes('sticky_wall'))
				{
					isStickyRenderer = false;
					isStickyVisible = false;
					document.querySelector(".close_sticky").style.display = "none";
				}
			});

			googletag.pubads().addEventListener('slotRenderEnded', (event) =>
			{
				if(event.slot.getAdUnitPath().includes('sticky_wall') && ESCheckMobileDevice())
				{
					isStickyRenderer = true;
				}
			});

							googletag.pubads().setTargeting('type', 'Category');
							googletag.pubads().setTargeting('key', '6666cd76f96956469e7be39d750cc7d9');
							googletag.pubads().setTargeting('page_url', 'https://www.muyinteresante.es');
							googletag.pubads().setTargeting('cabecera', 'muyinteresante');
							googletag.pubads().setTargeting('parent_category', 'inicio');
							googletag.pubads().setTargeting('category', 'inicio');
			
			googletag.pubads().set("page_url", location.origin + location.pathname);

			try {
				map="['"+cs_smart.replace(/cs=/g, "").replace(/;/g, "','")+"']";
				googletag.pubads().setTargeting('cs', map);
			}catch(error) {}

			googletag.pubads().addEventListener('impressionViewable', (event) => {
				if(event.slot.getAdUnitPath().includes('sticky_wall') && ESCheckMobileDevice())
				{
					isStickyVisible = true;
				}
			});

			googletag.pubads().enableSingleRequest();
			googletag.pubads().disableInitialLoad();
			googletag.enableServices();

			AdsToCall.forEach( ad => {

				if(ad.action === AD_DISPLAY )
				{
					console.log("Calling late display in: " + ad.name);
					googletag.display(`${ad.name}`);
				}

				if(ad.action === AD_REFRESH )
				{
					console.log("Calling late refresh in: " + ad.name);
					googletag.pubads().refresh([getNameForRefresh(`${ad.name}`)]);
				}

				if(ad.action === AD_DISPLAY_AND_REFRESH )
				{
					console.log("Calling late display and refresh in: " + ad.name);
					googletag.display(`${ad.name}`);
					googletag.pubads().refresh([getNameForRefresh(`${ad.name}`)]);
				}
			});

			if(ESCheckMobileDevice())
			{
				StickyTimer = setInterval(() => {
					if(isStickyVisible && isStickyRenderer)
					{
						if(document.querySelector("#sticky_wall").querySelector("iframe"))
							if( +document.querySelector("#sticky_wall").querySelector("iframe").getAttribute("width") > 1 ) {
								document.querySelector(".close_sticky").style.display = "block";
								document.querySelector("#sideAds").style.opacity = "1";
							}
					}
				}, 3000);
			}

			adsStarted = true;
		});
	}

	function isMobileDevice()
	{
		let check = false;
		(function(a){if(/(android|bb\d+|meego).+mobile|avantgo|bada\/|blackberry|blazer|compal|elaine|fennec|hiptop|iemobile|ip(hone|od)|iris|kindle|lge |maemo|midp|mmp|mobile.+firefox|netfront|opera 	function filterRubiconWithDevice(key, value)
	{
		let tmpItem = {};

		if(key === "sticky")
		{
			tmpItem = { [key]: value };
			return tmpItem;
		}
		else
		{
			if(deviceIsMobile)
			{
				if(!key.includes("dsk"))
				{
					tmpItem = { [key.replace("_phn", "")]: value };
					return tmpItem;
				}
			}
			else
			{
				if(!key.includes("phn"))
				{
					tmpItem = { [key.replace("_dsk", "")]: value };
					return tmpItem;
				}
			}
		}

		return null;
	}

    function reloadSticky()
    {
		if(!AdsLaunched)
			return;

		}

    function addStilesStripe() {
        window.addEventListener("scroll", (event) => {
            let scroll = window.scrollY;
            scroll > 100
                ? stripeHeader.classList.add("stripeHeaderTop")
                : stripeHeader.classList.remove("stripeHeaderTop");
        });

        addStilesStripe();

           Nueva forma de generar electricidad a partir de la lluvia puede alimentar 100 bombillas LED por gota
          </a>

        <p class="box--summary text-center">

  <script>
   let timerIndigitall = null;

  function StartPopupIndigitall()
  {
    timerIndigitall = setInterval(PushNotificationsPopup, 4000);
  }

  function PushNotificationsPopup(mode = "auto")
  {
    let configStored = localStorage.getItem("ZinetPushNotificatiosnConfig");

    if(mode === "auto" && configStored != null)
    {
      clearInterval(timerIndigitall);
      return;
    }

    if(document.querySelector(".pushnotifications--popup"))
    {
      clearInterval(timerIndigitall);
      return;
    }

    if(Notification.permission !== "granted")
    {     
      if(document.querySelector("#NotificationsPopupToogle"))
        document.querySelector("#NotificationsPopupToogle").style.display = "none";
        
      return;
    }

    indigitall.deviceGet((device) => {
      indigitall.topicsList((topics) => {
            if(topics.length <= 0)
            return;
            
            let PushNotificationsPopupTemplate;

              GetTranslatedString("push_message", null, true).then(msg => {
                  PushNotificationsPopupTemplate = 
                  `
                  <div class="pushnotifications--popup--logo"><img src="/images/popup_login_header.png"></div>
                  <div class="pushnotifications--popup--text">${msg[0]}:</div>
                      <div class="pushnotifications--popup--list--container">
                          <ul class="pushnotifications--popup--list">
                              ${topics.map(topic => `
                                <li>
                                    <label>
                                      ${topic.name}
                                    </label>
                                    <input ${topic.subscribed ? "checked" : ""} data-push-topic type="checkbox" value="${topic.code}">
                                </li>`).join('')}
                          </ul>
                      </div>
                      <div class="pushnotifications--popup--buttons"><input class="pushnotifications--popup--save" id="pushnotifications--popup--save" type="button" value="${msg[1]}"></div>            
                  </div>
                  `;          

                  const tempDiv = document.createElement('div');
                  tempDiv.className = "pushnotifications--popup";
                  tempDiv.innerHTML = PushNotificationsPopupTemplate;
                  document.querySelector("body").insertAdjacentElement("afterbegin", tempDiv);

                  clearInterval(timerIndigitall);                  

                  document.querySelector("#pushnotifications--popup--save").addEventListener("click", ()=>
                  {
                    let topicsInputs = document.querySelectorAll("[data-push-topic]");
                    let tmpValuesEnabled  = [];
                    let tmpValuesDisabled = [];

                    for(let topic of topicsInputs)
                    {
                      tmpValuesDisabled.push(topic.value);
                    }

                    indigitall.topicsUnsubscribe(tmpValuesDisabled, (topics) => {

                      for(let topic of topicsInputs)
                      {
                        if(topic.checked === true)
                        {
                          tmpValuesEnabled.push(topic.value);
                        }
                      }

                      indigitall.topicsSubscribe(tmpValuesEnabled); 

                    }, () => {
                      console.log("Couldn´t unsubscribe to topics");
                    });

                    document.querySelector(".pushnotifications--popup").remove();

                    if(mode === "auto")
                      localStorage.setItem("ZinetPushNotificatiosnConfig", "stored");
                  });

              });
          }, 
          () => {
              console.log("Couldn´t retrieve topics from Indigitall");
          });
    },() => {
      console.log("Couldn´t find a device");
    });
  }

  async function GetTranslatedString(key, target = null, multiline = false)
  {
    let isDevelopment = location.href.includes("app_dev.php");
    let cleanedURL    = location.hostname.replace("backend", "");
    let finalURL      = `${location.protocol}//${cleanedURL}${(isDevelopment ? "/app_dev.php" : "")}/translations/${key}`;

    let myHeaders = new Headers();
    myHeaders.append('X-Requested-With', 'XMLHttpRequest');

    let myInit = { method: 'GET', headers: myHeaders, mode: 'cors', cache: 'default' };
    let firstResponse = await fetch(finalURL, myInit);
    let parsedJSON    = await firstResponse.json();

    if(!target)
    {
      if(multiline)
      {
        return parsedJSON[key].split("|");
      }
      else
      {
        return parsedJSON[key];
      }
    }
    else
      document.querySelector(target).innerHTML = parsedJSON[key];
  }
  </script>
